<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предавать.html>предава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predavátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предаться.html>преда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give oneself up <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнев.html>гне́ву</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:страсть.html>страстя́м</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predavátʹsja</b> gnévu (strastjám)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give oneself up (abandon oneself) to anger (passions)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́янию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predavátʹsja</b> otčájaniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give way to despair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порок.html>поро́кам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predavátʹsja</b> porókam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to indulge in vices</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечта.html>мечта́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predavátʹsja</b> mečtám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into a reverie; lapse into daydreams</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предавать.html>предава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unreliable</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предательство.html>преда́тельство</a> (5615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предатель.html>преда́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predátelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предательство.html>преда́тельство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predátelʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предательство.html>преда́тельства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предательство.html>преда́тельства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предательство.html>преда́тельств</a></b>)

***предать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предать.html>преда́ть</a> (5539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*perdati</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*per-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dati</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передать.html>переда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предать.html>преда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предаться.html>преда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give oneself up <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаться.html>преда́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнев.html>гне́ву</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:страсть.html>страстя́м</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predátʹsja</b> gnévu (strastjám)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give oneself up (abandon oneself) to anger (passions)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаться.html>преда́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́янию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predátʹsja</b> otčájaniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give way to despair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаться.html>преда́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порок.html>поро́кам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predátʹsja</b> porókam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to indulge in vices</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаться.html>преда́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечта.html>мечта́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predátʹsja</b> mečtám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into a reverie; lapse into daydreams</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предать.html>преда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***предающийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предающийся.html>предаю́щийся</a> (10675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***предварить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предварить.html>предвари́ть</a> (30733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварить.html>предвари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predvarítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварять.html>предваря́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forestall, to anticipate</li>
<li>to premise <i>(with)</i>, to begin <i>(by)</i></li>
<li>to tell beforehand <i>(about)</i>, (fore)to warn <i>(of)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предваряемый.html>предваря́емый</a> (29736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предваряемый.html>предваря́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predvarjájemyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предварять.html>предваря́ть</a> (29736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварить.html>предвари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predvarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварять.html>предваря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predvarjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварить.html>предвари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forestall, to anticipate</li>
<li>to premise <i>(with)</i>, to begin <i>(by)</i></li>
<li>to tell beforehand <i>(about)</i>, (fore)to warn <i>(of)</i></li></ol>

***предвещать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предвещать.html>предвеща́ть</a> (12965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предвещать.html>предвеща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predveščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to forebode, to presage, to portend, to betoken, to foretoken, to foreshadow, to herald, to augur</li></ol>

***предвидеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предвидеть.html>предви́деть</a> (6362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́деть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vídetʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предвидеть.html>предви́деть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predvídetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to foresee, to foreknow</li></ol>

***предвкушение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предвкушение.html>предвкуше́ние</a> (14449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">предвкуси́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predvkusítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предвкушение.html>предвкуше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predvkušénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предвкушение.html>предвкуше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предвкушение.html>предвкуше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предвкушение.html>предвкуше́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>anticipation, foretaste</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́л</a> (1428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predél</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>limit, boundary, margin</li>
<li>border</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> precincts</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> limit</li></ol>
